    66  	Describe(`Service constructor tests using external config`, func() {
    67  		Context(`Using external config, construct service client instances`, func() {
    68  			// Map containing environment variables used in testing.
    69  			var testEnvironment = map[string]string{
    70  				"FINDINGS_URL":       "https://findingsv1/api",
    71  				"FINDINGS_AUTH_TYPE": "noauth",
    72  			}
    73  
    74  			It(`Create service client using external config successfully`, func() {
    75  				SetTestEnvironment(testEnvironment)
    76  				findingsService, serviceErr := findingsv1.NewFindingsV1UsingExternalConfig(&findingsv1.FindingsV1Options{})
    77  				Expect(findingsService).ToNot(BeNil())
    78  				Expect(serviceErr).To(BeNil())
    79  				ClearTestEnvironment(testEnvironment)
    80  
    81  				clone := findingsService.Clone()
    82  				Expect(clone).ToNot(BeNil())
    83  				Expect(clone.Service != findingsService.Service).To(BeTrue())
    84  				Expect(clone.GetServiceURL()).To(Equal(findingsService.GetServiceURL()))
    85  				Expect(clone.Service.Options.Authenticator).To(Equal(findingsService.Service.Options.Authenticator))
    86  			})

   100  				Expect(clone.GetServiceURL()).To(Equal(findingsService.GetServiceURL()))
   101  				Expect(clone.Service.Options.Authenticator).To(Equal(findingsService.Service.Options.Authenticator))
   102  			})

   154  	Describe(`Regional endpoint tests`, func() {
   155  		It(`GetServiceURLForRegion(region string)`, func() {
   156  			var url string
   157  			var err error
   158  			url, err = findingsv1.GetServiceURLForRegion("us-south")
   159  			Expect(url).To(Equal("https://us-south.secadvisor.cloud.ibm.com/findings"))
   160  			Expect(err).To(BeNil())
   161  
   162  			url, err = findingsv1.GetServiceURLForRegion("us-east")
   163  			Expect(url).To(Equal("https://us-south.secadvisor.cloud.ibm.com/findings"))
   164  			Expect(err).To(BeNil())
   165  
   166  			url, err = findingsv1.GetServiceURLForRegion("eu-gb")
   167  			Expect(url).To(Equal("https://eu-gb.secadvisor.cloud.ibm.com/findings"))
   168  			Expect(err).To(BeNil())
   169  
   170  			url, err = findingsv1.GetServiceURLForRegion("eu-de")
   171  			Expect(url).To(Equal("https://eu.compliance.cloud.ibm.com/si/findings"))
   172  			Expect(err).To(BeNil())
   173  
   174  			url, err = findingsv1.GetServiceURLForRegion("INVALID_REGION")
   175  			Expect(url).To(BeEmpty())
   176  			Expect(err).ToNot(BeNil())
   177  			fmt.Fprintf(GinkgoWriter, "Expected error: %s\n", err.Error())
   178  		})
   179  	})
   180  	Describe(`PostGraph(postGraphOptions *PostGraphOptions)`, func() {
   181  		postGraphPath := "/v1/testString/graph"
   182  		Context(`Using mock server endpoint`, func() {
   183  			BeforeEach(func() {
   184  				testServer = httptest.NewServer(http.HandlerFunc(func(res http.ResponseWriter, req *http.Request) {
   185  					defer GinkgoRecover()
   186  
   187  					// Verify the contents of the request
   188  					Expect(req.URL.EscapedPath()).To(Equal(postGraphPath))
   189  					Expect(req.Method).To(Equal("POST"))
   190  
   191  					// For gzip-disabled operation, verify Content-Encoding is not set.
   192  					Expect(req.Header.Get("Content-Encoding")).To(BeEmpty())
   193  
   194  					// If there is a body, then make sure we can read it
   195  					bodyBuf := new(bytes.Buffer)
   196  					if req.Header.Get("Content-Encoding") == "gzip" {
   197  						body, err := core.NewGzipDecompressionReader(req.Body)
   198  						Expect(err).To(BeNil())
   199  						_, err = bodyBuf.ReadFrom(body)
   200  						Expect(err).To(BeNil())
   201  					} else {
   202  						_, err := bodyBuf.ReadFrom(req.Body)
   203  						Expect(err).To(BeNil())
   204  					}
   205  					fmt.Fprintf(GinkgoWriter, "  Request body: %s", bodyBuf.String())
   206  
   207  					Expect(req.Header["Content-Type"]).ToNot(BeNil())
   208  					Expect(req.Header["Content-Type"][0]).To(Equal(fmt.Sprintf("%v", "application/json")))
   209  					Expect(req.Header["Transaction-Id"]).ToNot(BeNil())
   210  					Expect(req.Header["Transaction-Id"][0]).To(Equal(fmt.Sprintf("%v", "testString")))
   211  					res.WriteHeader(200)
   212  				}))
   213  			})
   214  			It(`Invoke PostGraph successfully`, func() {
   215  				findingsService, serviceErr := findingsv1.NewFindingsV1(&findingsv1.FindingsV1Options{
   216  					URL:           testServer.URL,
   217  					Authenticator: &core.NoAuthAuthenticator{},
   218  				})
   219  				Expect(serviceErr).To(BeNil())
   220  				Expect(findingsService).ToNot(BeNil())
   221  
   222  				// Invoke operation with nil options model (negative test)
   223  				response, operationErr := findingsService.PostGraph(nil)
   224  				Expect(operationErr).NotTo(BeNil())
   225  				Expect(response).To(BeNil())
   226  
   227  				// Construct an instance of the PostGraphOptions model
   228  				postGraphOptionsModel := new(findingsv1.PostGraphOptions)
   229  				postGraphOptionsModel.AccountID = core.StringPtr("testString")
   230  				postGraphOptionsModel.Body = CreateMockReader("This is a mock file.")
   231  				postGraphOptionsModel.ContentType = core.StringPtr("application/json")
   232  				postGraphOptionsModel.TransactionID = core.StringPtr("testString")
   233  				postGraphOptionsModel.Headers = map[string]string{"x-custom-header": "x-custom-value"}
   234  
   235  				// Invoke operation with valid options model (positive test)
   236  				response, operationErr = findingsService.PostGraph(postGraphOptionsModel)
   237  				Expect(operationErr).To(BeNil())
   238  				Expect(response).ToNot(BeNil())
   239  			})
   240  			It(`Invoke PostGraph with error: Operation validation and request error`, func() {
   241  				findingsService, serviceErr := findingsv1.NewFindingsV1(&findingsv1.FindingsV1Options{
   242  					URL:           testServer.URL,
   243  					Authenticator: &core.NoAuthAuthenticator{},
   244  				})
   245  				Expect(serviceErr).To(BeNil())
   246  				Expect(findingsService).ToNot(BeNil())
   247  
   248  				// Construct an instance of the PostGraphOptions model
   249  				postGraphOptionsModel := new(findingsv1.PostGraphOptions)
   250  				postGraphOptionsModel.AccountID = core.StringPtr("testString")
   251  				postGraphOptionsModel.Body = CreateMockReader("This is a mock file.")
   252  				postGraphOptionsModel.ContentType = core.StringPtr("application/json")
   253  				postGraphOptionsModel.TransactionID = core.StringPtr("testString")
   254  				postGraphOptionsModel.Headers = map[string]string{"x-custom-header": "x-custom-value"}
   255  				// Invoke operation with empty URL (negative test)
   256  				err := findingsService.SetServiceURL("")
   257  				Expect(err).To(BeNil())
   258  				response, operationErr := findingsService.PostGraph(postGraphOptionsModel)
   259  				Expect(operationErr).ToNot(BeNil())
   260  				Expect(operationErr.Error()).To(ContainSubstring(core.ERRORMSG_SERVICE_URL_MISSING))
   261  				Expect(response).To(BeNil())
   262  				// Construct a second instance of the PostGraphOptions model with no property values
   263  				postGraphOptionsModelNew := new(findingsv1.PostGraphOptions)
   264  				// Invoke operation with invalid model (negative test)
   265  				response, operationErr = findingsService.PostGraph(postGraphOptionsModelNew)
   266  				Expect(operationErr).ToNot(BeNil())
   267  				Expect(response).To(BeNil())
   268  			})
   269  			AfterEach(func() {
   270  				testServer.Close()
   271  			})
   272  		})
   273  	})

   391  	Describe(`CreateNote(createNoteOptions *CreateNoteOptions)`, func() {
   392  		createNotePath := "/v1/testString/providers/testString/notes"
   393  		Context(`Using mock server endpoint with timeout`, func() {
   394  			BeforeEach(func() {
   395  				testServer = httptest.NewServer(http.HandlerFunc(func(res http.ResponseWriter, req *http.Request) {
   396  					defer GinkgoRecover()
   397  
   398  					// Verify the contents of the request
   399  					Expect(req.URL.EscapedPath()).To(Equal(createNotePath))
   400  					Expect(req.Method).To(Equal("POST"))
   401  
   402  					// For gzip-disabled operation, verify Content-Encoding is not set.
   403  					Expect(req.Header.Get("Content-Encoding")).To(BeEmpty())
   404  
   405  					// If there is a body, then make sure we can read it
   406  					bodyBuf := new(bytes.Buffer)
   407  					if req.Header.Get("Content-Encoding") == "gzip" {
   408  						body, err := core.NewGzipDecompressionReader(req.Body)
   409  						Expect(err).To(BeNil())
   410  						_, err = bodyBuf.ReadFrom(body)
   411  						Expect(err).To(BeNil())
   412  					} else {
   413  						_, err := bodyBuf.ReadFrom(req.Body)
   414  						Expect(err).To(BeNil())
   415  					}
   416  					fmt.Fprintf(GinkgoWriter, "  Request body: %s", bodyBuf.String())
   417  
   418  					Expect(req.Header["Transaction-Id"]).ToNot(BeNil())
   419  					Expect(req.Header["Transaction-Id"][0]).To(Equal(fmt.Sprintf("%v", "testString")))
   420  					// Sleep a short time to support a timeout test
   421  					time.Sleep(100 * time.Millisecond)
   422  
   423  					// Set mock response
   424  					res.Header().Set("Content-type", "application/json")
   425  					res.WriteHeader(200)
   426  					fmt.Fprintf(res, "%s", `{"short_description": "ShortDescription", "long_description": "LongDescription", "kind": "FINDING", "related_url": [{"label": "Label", "url": "URL"}], "expiration_time": "2019-01-01T12:00:00.000Z", "create_time": "2019-01-01T12:00:00.000Z", "update_time": "2019-01-01T12:00:00.000Z", "id": "ID", "shared": true, "reported_by": {"id": "ID", "title": "Title", "url": "URL"}, "finding": {"severity": "LOW", "next_steps": [{"title": "Title", "url": "URL"}]}, "kpi": {"aggregation_type": "SUM"}, "card": {"section": "Section", "title": "Title", "subtitle": "Subtitle", "order": 1, "finding_note_names": ["FindingNoteNames"], "requires_configuration": false, "badge_text": "BadgeText", "badge_image": "BadgeImage", "elements": [{"text": "Text", "default_interval": "DefaultInterval", "kind": "TIME_SERIES", "default_time_range": "1d", "value_types": [{"kind": "FINDING_COUNT", "finding_note_names": ["FindingNoteNames"], "text": "Text"}]}]}, "section": {"title": "Title", "image": "Image"}}`)
   427  				}))
   428  			})
   429  			It(`Invoke CreateNote successfully with retries`, func() {
   430  				findingsService, serviceErr := findingsv1.NewFindingsV1(&findingsv1.FindingsV1Options{
   431  					URL:           testServer.URL,
   432  					Authenticator: &core.NoAuthAuthenticator{},
   433  				})
   434  				Expect(serviceErr).To(BeNil())
   435  				Expect(findingsService).ToNot(BeNil())
   436  				findingsService.EnableRetries(0, 0)

   541  					defer GinkgoRecover()
   542  
   543  					// Verify the contents of the request
   544  					Expect(req.URL.EscapedPath()).To(Equal(createNotePath))

   549

   551  					bodyBuf := new(bytes.Buffer)
   552  					if req.Header.Get("Content-Encoding") == "gzip" {
   553  						body, err := core.NewGzipDecompressionReader(req.Body)
   554  						Expect(err).To(BeNil())
   555  						_, err = bodyBuf.ReadFrom(body)
   556  						Expect(err).To(BeNil())
   557  					} else {
   558  						_, err := bodyBuf.ReadFrom(req.Body)
   559  						Expect(err).To(BeNil())
   560  					}

   971  				defer cancelFunc()

   973  				Expect(operationErr).ToNot(BeNil())

   980  				Expect(response).ToNot(BeNil())
   981  				Expect(result).ToNot(BeNil())
   982

   987  				Expect(operationErr).ToNot(BeNil())
   988  				Expect(operationErr.Error()).To(ContainSubstring("deadline exceeded"))

  5309  func CreateMockByteArray(mockData string) *[]byte {
  5310  	ba := make([]byte, 0)
  5311  	ba = append(ba, mockData...)
  5312  	return &ba
  5313  }

  5316  	uuid := strfmt.UUID(mockData)

  5318  }

  5320  func CreateMockReader(mockData string) io.ReadCloser {
  5321  	return ioutil.NopCloser(bytes.NewReader([]byte(mockData)))
  5322  }

  5324  func CreateMockDate(mockData string) *strfmt.Date {

  5327  		return nil
  5328  	}
  5329  	return &d
  5330  }
